      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 17th century
       </b>
       . During the period 1601 to 1700 there were 248 solar eclipses of which 89 were partial, 74 were annular, 61 were total (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), and 24 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 16 different years: 1613, 1620, 1624, 1631, 1638, 1642, 1649, 1653, 1660, 1667, 1671, 1678, 1685, 1689, 1693, and 1696. Two months, May 1631 and May 1696, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
